FACILITY   (LINAC,2ZZZGEL) GELINA facility.                       23137  1   29 
            Gamma Array for Inelastic Neutron Scattering (GAINS)  23137  1   30 
            setup.                                                23137  1   31 
            Neutron source was operated at 800Hz repetition rate  23137  1   32 
           providing pulses of o1 ns FWHM.                        23137  1   33 
INC-SOURCE Primary neutron production target is depleted uranium  23137  1   34 
            (U-10Mo alloy). Time resolution primary beam - 1ns.   23137  1   35 
           Angle relative to electron beam - 90 deg.              23137  1   36 
           Beam diameter 61 mm.                                   23137  1   37 
METHOD     (TOF) For incident neutron energy. Flight path 198.7m. 23137  1   38 
            (n,n'gamma) technique - for high resolution scattering23137  1   39 
           data. Neutron energy resolution of about 1keV at 1MeV. 23137  1   40 
           The data acquisition for the HPGe detectors was made   23137  1   41 
           with Acquiris DC440 digitizers with 12bit amplitude    23137  1   42 
           resolution and sampling rate of 440 million samples/s. 23137  1   43 
DETECTOR   (HPGE) 7 large volume high purity germanium (HPGe)     23137  1   44 
           Canberra detectors of 8cm diameter,8cm long;           23137  1   45 
           positioned at angles of 110 and 150 deg to the beam,   23137  1   46 
           at distances of 14-16.5cm from the target.             23137  1   47 
            Typical gamma energy resolution of 2.3keV for the     23137  1   48 
           1.332MeV peak of Co-60.                                23137  1   49 
            Eu-152 point source (PTB-6.11-108-97, activity 42.9(3)23137  1   50 
           kBq on 1/6/1997) was used for calibration.             23137  1   51 
           The measured efficiencies of 11 152-Eu gamma-rays of   23137  1   52 
           energies 245-1408 keV were used for the tests of the   23137  1   53 
           geometrical model (based on MCNP simulation of the     23137  1   54 
           complete setup) for each detector. Average agreement of23137  1   55 
           1.70% between the calculated and the experimental      23137  1   56 
           values of efficiency.                                  23137  1   57 
           Detailed exp. efficiencies of each detector are given  23137  1   58 
           in Table 4 of J,NIM/A,672,82,2012 for E-gammas 440,    23137  1   59 
           1636, 2264, 2391, 2542, 2640 keV.                      23137  1   60 
           (FISCH) U-235 fission chamber located at 147.5cm       23137  1   61 
           upstream from the target, operated in parallel with the23137  1   62 
           HPGe setup - for neutron fluence measurement.          23137  1   63 
           Fission chamber contains an assembly of 8 UF4 deposits 23137  1   64 
           of 70+/-0.2 mm diameter, evaporated on five Al foils of23137  1   65 
           20 microm thickness.                                   23137  1   66 
           Thickness of the UF4 deposits of the fission chamber:  23137  1   67 
           Foil                  Thickness(microg/cm**2)          23137  1   68 
                                 U          U-235      UF4        23137  1   69 
           Target 1 side 1       422(3)     421(3)     558(3)     23137  1   70 
           Target 2 side 1       419(2)     419(2)     555(3)     23137  1   71 
           Target 3 side 1       421(3)     421(3)     558(3)     23137  1   72 
           Target 1 side 2       383(2)     383(2)     507(3)     23137  1   73 
           Target 2 side 2       383(2)     382(2)     507(3)     23137  1   74 
           Target 3 side 2       383(2)     382(2)     507(3)     23137  1   75 
           Target 4              327(2)     326(2)     432(3)     23137  1   76 
           Target 6              327(2)     327(2)     433(2)     23137  1   77 
           Total                 3066(6)    3061(6)    4058(8)    23137  1   78 
           The amounts of U and 235U deposits were determined by  23137  1   79 
           alpha counting.                                        23137  1   80 
           The P10 gas in the chamber is kept at atmospheric      23137  1   81 
           pressure.                                              23137  1   82 
           Efficiency 83. +/- 1. %.                               23137  1   83 
           The technique for the determination of the neutron     23137  1   84 
           detection efficiency was revised according to the      23137  1   85 
           methodology described in REL-REF of D.B.Gayther and    23137  1   86 
           tests performed at the IRMM Van de Graaff accelerator  23137  1   87 
           during 2009. The method was subsequently validated by  23137  1   88 
           an instrument intercomparison carried out at PTB,      23137  1   89 
           during which the neutron sensitivity of the fission    23137  1   90 
           chamber(FP3/200m) was found to agree within one        23137  1   91 
           standard deviation with the PTB proton recoil          23137  1   92 
           telescope RPT1.                                        23137  1   93 
           Resulting efficiency of fission chamber (83+-1) % .    23137  1   94 
SAMPLE     - Na metallic sample(TP-NP08/10) was prepared at IRMM  23137  1   95 
           from sodium ingot of elemental purity 99.8%, supplied  23137  1   96 
           by Alpha Aesar. The material was formed by cutting     23137  1   97 
           under argon atmosphere, rolling and punching under oil 23137  1   98 
           into a cylindrical disk of 79.80+-0.08 mm diameter,    23137  1   99 
           4.23+-0.08mm thickness and a mass of 19.44+-0.04 g;    23137  1  100 
           enclosed in an Al can of 0.50+-0.01 mm wall thickness. 23137  1  101 
           Sample had a density of 0.92 g/cm**3, 95% of the       23137  1  102 
           theoretical density of metallic sodium(0.97g/cm**3).   23137  1  103 
           Mass per unit area 0.389(1)g/cm**2.                    23137  1  104 
           The sample diameter is larger than beam diameter(61mm).23137  1  105 
           -Isotopic composition(atoms%)of the UF4 deposits of the23137  1  106 
           fission chamber:                                       23137  1  107 
           U-234 - 0.0628+-0.0025, U-235 - 99.8268+-0.0044,       23137  1  108 
           U-236 - 0.0365+-0.0027, U-238 - 0.0739+-0.0025.        23137  1  109
